Above is a multi-hour APRS capture, where no-printables are replace by [hex codes in brackets], or FEND or FESQ or TFEND or TESC.

Another packet, after processing FESC:

[0x00][0x82][0xA0][0x9E][0xA8]db[0xE0][0x96][0xB2]n[0x88][0xA4]@[0xE8][0xAE]h[0x86][0xA6][0x8E]@[0xE0][0xAE][0x92][0x88][0x8A]d@a[0x03][0xF0]!3228.50N/08456.90W# 13.0V  20C  ky7dr.com P1

[0x00] command, 0 = data packet
[0x82] - should be flag with value 0x7E, which it obviously isn't
[0xA0][0x9E][0xA8]db[0xE0][0x96] - should be dest address, 7 bytes
[0xB2]n[0x88][0xA4]@[0xE8][0xAE] - should be source address, 7 bytes
h[0x86][0xA6][0x8E]@[0xE0][0xAE][0x92][0x88][0x8A]d@a[0x03] - digipeater addresses, 0-8 digipeaters comma-separated, 0-56 bytes
[0xF0] protocol ID, 0xF0 means no layer 3 protocol
Everything else is APRS data in the "Information Field" (followed by FCS = frame check sequence, a checksum of some type)
!3228.50N/08456.90W# 13.0V  20C  ky7dr.com P1
